<span id="freeTextContainer8695728516981430147"><br/>★★★☆ <b>3.5 Stars!</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1399123063i/9510760.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I guess this was another one of those <b>
  <i>"I liked it but didn't love it"</i>
</b> type of books, mainly because there was so much:<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1399123837ra/9510993.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Maybe my expectations were a bit too high or maybe I just wasn't really in the mood for the constant angst/tension that was happening in this book, but I wasn't as invested in the story as I was hoping to be.<br/><br/>Don't get me wrong; there were some definite 4 star-worth scenes. There was an interesting back story, fun side characters, alternating POV's, a feisty her</span>
  <span id="freeText8695728516981430147" style="display:none"><br>★★★☆ <b>3.5 Stars!</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1399123063i/9510760.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I guess this was another one of those <b>
  <i>"I liked it but didn't love it"</i>
</b> type of books, mainly because there was so much:<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1399123837ra/9510993.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Maybe my expectations were a bit too high or maybe I just wasn't really in the mood for the constant angst/tension that was happening in this book, but I wasn't as invested in the story as I was hoping to be.<br><br>Don't get me wrong; there were some definite 4 star-worth scenes. There was an interesting back story, fun side characters, alternating POV's, a feisty heroine and a tattooed/pierced bad boy hero. What's not to like about all of that, right? <br><br>Well, there's also the fact that the book (at least the version I had of it) needs some major editing. I don't mind it at all when there are just a few spelling mistakes, but when they appear on almost every other page and when there's a huge lack of punctuation, it becomes a bit distracting...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1386945307ra/7489132.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I think, if I'd read this book a year and a half ago I would have probably enjoyed it much more. But now it seems as if I've read so many NA "good girl falls for tortured man-whore hero" stories that it takes a lot for me to be blown away by one... Still, it was overall a fun read and I'll most likely continue with the rest of the series...<b>Jet, Rome and Nash</b> have already sparked my interest so I'm looking forward to read their stories ;)<br><br>My favorite quote:<br><br><blockquote>
<i>"Me and this girl spent too much time trying to be too many different things for too many wrong reasons for too many other people, now it was just up to us to be ourselves for each other and love each other for all the right reasons."</i>♥</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1399123063i/9510761.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

<div id="review_813749778" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/813749778" />
    <a title="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/17755575-wendy-sthoughts"><img alt="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1378340325p2/17755575.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/813749778?book_show_action=true">Jan 05, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" href="/user/show/17755575-wendy-sthoughts">Wendy&#39;sThoughts</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer813749778" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7422567610665896933"><b>4.5 Pierced, Tatted, Mohawked, Forever Stars<br/>* * * * 1/2 <i>Spoiler Free-2014 Review</i><br/>Due to my wonderful GR pals... a book called Rome came across my feed. Read the reviews/teasers and found out it was part of the Marked Men series by Jay Crownover. Being that I like to look into the source or beginning of a series even if they are stand-alone... found out the first part of this group was Rule. So off I went to meet him, his family and friends.<br/><br/>Well, I was in for a treat. </b>I met a fella who was torture</span>
  <span id="freeText7422567610665896933" style="display:none"><b>4.5 Pierced, Tatted, Mohawked, Forever Stars<br>* * * * 1/2 <i>Spoiler Free-2014 Review</i><br>Due to my wonderful GR pals... a book called Rome came across my feed. Read the reviews/teasers and found out it was part of the Marked Men series by Jay Crownover. Being that I like to look into the source or beginning of a series even if they are stand-alone... found out the first part of this group was Rule. So off I went to meet him, his family and friends.<br><br>Well, I was in for a treat. </b>I met a fella who was tortured, hot, confident in spite of everything, and had that special something that made anyone with a vagina want him... no questions asked and under any conditions. <br><br>He was part of a family which on the surface functioned before the tragedy happened killing his twin, Remy. This family had Rome, the eldest and keeper of them all in line; with Remy the "good, amiable, peace-keeper twin and Rule fulfilling the slot of difficult, stubborn, marching to his own drum and banging it loudly. The parents of these children were everyday people...living their lives and seeming to be the answer to a little lost girl's prayers.<br><br>This shy, emotionally poor girl from the ultra-rich parentage was found by Remy when she was 13... and he kept her safe, comforted, and became her lifeline to this family she wished was hers. <br><br>But what was the most precious for her in meeting these people was Rule... she was taken at first glance and continued to love him desperately. Remy knew she did... but somewhere in the bonding of Remy and Shaw, an unwritten contract was formed of a knowing which would be hidden from all ... and no matter how many times Shaw explained to the family, Remy and she were Not lovers, just the very best of friends... no one believed her...especially Rule... as Shaw was everything he never would have... clean, privileged, super smart and his twin brother's girl.<br><br>So they grow up together.. high school and then onto life... Tattooing, a career, and man whoring for Rule; Rome deciding the Army and protecting his country for him; Remy finding his place and him encouraging Shaw to come to Denver and college to be close to him and Rule.<br><br>Then that tragedy I mentioned happens... skewing everything... this perfect family, connections and how people relate to one another... <br>Remy dies driving to pick up Rule because he is drunk... and now Rule has heard out loud all of the venom from his mother's lips she has held back ....blaming him and saying at the grave, she wished it had been Rule... <br><br>So we meet these people at this juncture... doing a charade of life; Rule acting like he has it handled; fucking and drinking to ease the pain... Rome in the Army dealing with seeing all of his buddies dying around him and just trying to keep it together... and Shaw... <br><br>Shaw is the glue that is holding everyone connected by the tenuous threads left. She picks Rule up every Sunday in a war dance they have perfected; she coming and pulling him out the bed no matter what the flavor of the night was... getting him to his parents' house for Sunday brunch... living through the batting the mother and father do to Rule and her balancing everything because even as bad as all this is... it is not a fraction of how horrible her actual parents are... <br><br>Her actual parents either wish to pawn her off as a political prize to this Judge's son, Gabe... with no care as to whether she wants to be with him or his fucked up actions. They hold her tuition over her head to make her stay in line and Shaw wants to be an ER doctor... and make a difference in the world. She loads herself up with all of the classes, study groups, and a job just to get by. She doesn't pay attention to the fact she is stunningly beautiful... she only knows she has goals and the one she dreams of and thinks will never happen is Rule.<br><br>This book was an eye-opener for me... as a parent... My children are grown and yes, there were times all of us were frustrated with each other... but no matter the issues ... no matter the actions... my children knew their parents were their safe haven... that there were unconditional love and support... and in my naivete... I sometimes forget that is not always the case.<br><br>I forget... life other than my own, causes people to do and say things I could never consider thinking. I forget....people are raised, grow and never learn to not to trust because there has never been an example for them to see it is ok to do so.... and I forget that if you think you have never been loved... you may not know what that feeling is... and know how to accept it from others.<br><br>Rule... was that man/child who had the love and trust from his brothers... but that feeling from his parents ... not so much... so when Shaw and Rule finally connect the way everyone around them knows they should have years ago.... it is staggering to Rule... this feeling and he has to learn how to handle it... it is frightening... it is scary and he really doesn't want to fuck it up. <br><br>When these two connect... it is a thing of beauty... hot, frantic, wanting and just really good. Every time, the telling of their meeting together works... so this was an added bonus to a heartfelt couple.<br><br>Shaw was a great character... even in her most compliant and appeasing with her demanding and controlling parents... she showed an inner strength... she had a solid core of beliefs and although she may have faltered a couple of times... she always was strong in her love of Rule. She really saw him and his loyalty to his friends and brothers... she saw his creativity and talent ... and fought for him.<br><br>This story has all of the elements to love...extremely strong secondary characters; a plot and story to hold you, and the emotional kick which hits every chord sincerely... not manipulative in any way. <br><br>This book was an all niter for me...I started it in the late afternoon and before I realized it... it was well into late-night... I just couldn't let go of the ride I was on. <br><br>Thank you Lisa Jayne and Lili... because of you I discovered a terrific series and will be seeing if Jet and Ayden figure out their story... <br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17200687.Rule__Marked_Men___1_" title="Rule (Marked Men, #1) by Jay Crownover" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/books/1357012113l/17200687._SX50_.jpg" alt="Rule (Marked Men, #1) by Jay Crownover" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <b>Rule (Marked Men, #1) <br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/813749778">https://www.goodreads.com/review/show...</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17204860.Jet__Marked_Men___2_" title="Jet (Marked Men, #2) by Jay Crownover" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/books/1367338347l/17204860._SY75_.jpg" alt="Jet (Marked Men, #2) by Jay Crownover" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a> Jett (Marked Men, #2)<br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/814733957">https://www.goodreads.com/review/show...</a><br><a     <a title="NiCoLeTa E. {Addicted To Books}" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/37314676-nicoleta-e-addicted-to-books"><img alt="NiCoLeTa E. {Addicted To Books}" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1528808758p2/37314676.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

Those two people was so opposite in every possible way but in a strange way they were so perfect for each other!!! <br>Their story managed to earn a special spot inside my heart...<br>And i can not wait to find out more about all the others... <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380800461ra/3123556.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>But let me talk to you about Rule and Shaw first...<br><br><i>What can i say about Rule???</i><br>Rule was the ultimate badass, womanizer type... He was covered all over his body with tattoos and many piercings... But don't let his appearance to trick you... Inside of him was more depth than that!!! And what was the deal with all these tattoos??? First of all, he was an artist... a tattoo artist and he was living with his best friend. He liked to hook up with random girls and to get buzzed from time to time with alchool... He was in distance with his own family and not without a reason!!!<br><br>Three years before he was having a twin brother, but not anymore... His brother was the good guy, the guy that everybody loved... They were so similar in appearance, that's why he started to marking his body... To difference himself from his brother that loved so much. His loss cost him, and that loss was the reason that the relationship with his parents turned out to be an awful thing... The only person that tried so hard to built a bridge between him and his family was a girl that he barely could tolerate....<br><br>Shaw loved the Archer family like her own... No, more than her own!!! When she was thirteen Remy Archer saved her and took her under his wings and from that moment they were inseparable... So everyone around them assumed that they were a couple, but Shaw's heart was beating hard for his twin, Rule... Even though he was so untamed and independed... Even though he rarely acknowledge her presence... her heart belong to him!!! <br><br>And even though she lost her best friend, she still remained beside Rule and tried to make everything better for him... Even though her heart was breaking every time that she discovered a different girl in his bed or that he didn't want to have any kind of contact with her... <br><br>In that point, i would like to tell that Shaw was a great person with her own problems... Her parents were living in their own worlds and they only demanded things from her. They never show her love, they only made her do things that they wanted for their own good. So Shaw was dressing and acting like all the others wanted from her to do. And that was exhausting... <br>The only thing that she ever wanted for herself was Rule!!! <br>And one day, she claimed him and she managed to earn that battle... <br><br>But then started the problems.... <br>Problems with the parents, problems with her ex that he was the favorite person of her parents, problems with Rule...<br>You see, something started to change when Rule started to acknoledge her present as a woman... and because in all his life he was building walls around his heart, the feelings that surround him were so unfamiliar and so scary!!! <br>But Shaw knew him so well and she always accepted him the way he was... Something that nobody else was doing except her and his friends... <br><br>The journey of their relationship was long and sweet and difficult... but i guarantee you that it was a hell of a ride.... <br>A ride that i enjoyed so fuckin' much!!!<br><br>My only thorns in this book was that psycho ex of Shaw and Rule's mother... <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1433696457ra/15132406.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>What the hell was going on inside their minds???? That was unacceptable!!!<br><br>So, now Rule is over and i'm really wondering what else Jay had prepare from the rest of the guys!!! <br>I can not wait to find out!!!</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer6390975353801973631">I don't usually do "casting" but I couldn't resist this time.<br/><br/>Rule<br/><a href='http://s50.photobucket.com/albums/f339/vikkimathews/?action=view&current=050d18a83eaa5ea3c9c1a87de43d4016.jpg' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380404138i/786378._SY540_.jpg' alt='Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Shaw<br/><a href='http://s50.photobucket.com/albums/f339/vikkimathews/?action=view&current=3bf6946d366dc659c2ebe76c07c595d5.jpg' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380404138i/786379._SX540_.jpg' alt='Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><br/><br/>I didn't know what to expect going into this one, but I'm so glad I took a chance on it.<br/><br/>I loved Rule and Shaw. They were great characters. They were both battling some hard won demons, but managed to stay so appealing. <br/><br/>Rule is a hot bad boy. In some ways he reminded me of Brian from Rock Me. Tattoos artist, piercings, totally determined to live life in his own terms. <br/><br/><i> <b> "I think it's genetically impossible not to be kind</b></i></span>
  <span id="freeText6390975353801973631" style="display:none">I don't usually do "casting" but I couldn't resist this time.<br><br>Rule<br><a href="http://s50.photobucket.com/albums/f339/vikkimathews/?action=view&amp;current=050d18a83eaa5ea3c9c1a87de43d4016.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380404138i/786378._SY540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Shaw<br><a href="http://s50.photobucket.com/albums/f339/vikkimathews/?action=view&amp;current=3bf6946d366dc659c2ebe76c07c595d5.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380404138i/786379._SX540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br>I didn't know what to expect going into this one, but I'm so glad I took a chance on it.<br><br>I loved Rule and Shaw. They were great characters. They were both battling some hard won demons, but managed to stay so appealing. <br><br>Rule is a hot bad boy. In some ways he reminded me of Brian from Rock Me. Tattoos artist, piercings, totally determined to live life in his own terms. <br><br><i> <b> "I think it's genetically impossible not to be kind of in love with him when you come equipped with a vagina. It's just something about that angsty, moody swagger he has that makes you want to cuddle him up and make him feel better." </b> </i><br><br>On the surface, Shaw is his exact opposite. Where he could care less what anyone thinks, Shaw spends her life trying to please everyone else. Where Rule is all angsty and out of control emotions, Shaw is reserved, and a peacemaker. Rule is afraid to let anyone in. His "relationships" consist of a series of one night stands, which he uses to try and exercise his daemons. <br><br>Shaw and Rule have been connected for years though her relationship with his twin brother Remy. Three years after Remy's death, Shaw finally has the opportunity to have the one thing she has always wanted, just for her. Rule.<br><br>What follows was a beautiful story of two people finally growing up. Shaw finally learns that she needs to live for herself, and Rule learns that shutting everyone out and living only for yourself is the path to loneliness. <br><br>I loved every minute of this story. Neither of them were perfect. Both of them made mistakes. There was nothing easy about their relationship from having to battle their own issues, to crazy Ex's and family problems galore, but it was beautiful all the same.<br><br><i> <b> "She turned her head and kissed me on the temple. "Love you." I pressed my face into the curve where he neck met her shoulder and sucked the skin between my teeth. "I'm going to love you Shaw." Her eyes crinkled at the sides. "You already do." </b></i> <br><br>The secondary characters were all great too. I can't wait to read Jet's book next, and I'm really hoping that Rome gets a book of his own too.<br><br>Highly recommend. <br></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer2024237180894795615">3.5 stars. Honestly, y'all: Rule is a douche and a player. He tries his best to be everything his deceased perfect twin wasn't to the extremes. He sleeps with a different girl almost every day. He has his sexy body pierced and tatted (personally a fan of this rebellion :-p) Finally, his relationship with his parents is glacial. Shaw was his brother's best friend and Rule put her firmly on the off limits section. Except, he had no idea Shaw has loved him since she was 13. A drunken night makes al</span>
  <span id="freeText2024237180894795615" style="display:none">3.5 stars. Honestly, y'all: Rule is a douche and a player. He tries his best to be everything his deceased perfect twin wasn't to the extremes. He sleeps with a different girl almost every day. He has his sexy body pierced and tatted (personally a fan of this rebellion :-p) Finally, his relationship with his parents is glacial. Shaw was his brother's best friend and Rule put her firmly on the off limits section. Except, he had no idea Shaw has loved him since she was 13. A drunken night makes all those walls he has built to keep her out crumble to the heat they generate. These two have fantastic sexual chemistry. After it's all said and done, I was pleasantly surprised to read Rule bring the initial pursuer :) Dear Rule, however, is also learning to be in a relationship and goes about coping with his feelings in a very bad way. That part REALLY pissed me off. Almost as much as Shaw forgiving so easily. After that, they start to develop as a couple but hit a few big bumps along the way. I wasn't a fan of Rule's methods for coping, which consisted largely of ignoring Shaw or trying to change into what he thinks she wants, but it felt like a part of his flaws. I was really glad to read him finally come into himself. He shows good growth. I liked Shaw and her big heart. I wanted to put her in a bubble to protect her from the hurt that her family, ex, and sometimes Rule out her through. All in all a good read with a few cringe-worthy moments and plenty of steamy sexy times. Safety: No OM/Sharing, though there is major ex drama for the h. H kisses a OW. No rape. Yes to abuse but not by the H.<br /><br />PS: Started this in audio and finished in ebook. The ebook version was a grammar nazi's nightmare but I survived &gt;.&lt; lol</span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer513393637" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer17792339682497245390">4.5 Stars<br/><br/>Rule was a story you pick up and don’t want to put down. I’m always drawn to a story where unrequited love is finally returned, and Shaw has been in love with Rule since she was fourteen. Adding to the excitement, is a stalker ex boyfriend who won’t take no for an answer. <br/><br/><b>
  <i>I loved Rule like it was my mission in life. I loved him like it was inevitable, like no matter how many times I was shown what an awful idea it was, what a bad match we were, what a callous asshole he could be I co</i></b></span>
  <span id="freeText17792339682497245390" style="display:none">4.5 Stars<br /><br />Rule was a story you pick up and don’t want to put down. I’m always drawn to a story where unrequited love is finally returned, and Shaw has been in love with Rule since she was fourteen. Adding to the excitement, is a stalker ex boyfriend who won’t take no for an answer. <br /><br /><b>
  <i>I loved Rule like it was my mission in life. I loved him like it was inevitable, like no matter how many times I was shown what an awful idea it was, what a bad match we were, what a callous asshole he could be I couldn’t shake it. </i>
</b><br /><br />Shaw has been fixture in the Archer family since she was fourteen and Remy took her under his wing, but it’s always been Rule she’s been in love with. When Remy’s tragic death deals the family a blow, she’s determined to keep them together. She picks Rule up every Sunday for brunch with the family to make sure he goes. Each time she does, her heart breaks a little more having to witness the string of one night stands paraded in front of her every time. <br /><br />Rule has no idea that Shaw has loved him so long. He always assumed that Remy and Shaw were a couple, so he never paid much attention to her. Plus, she is the polar opposite to Rule. He’s all tatted and pierced up and does what he wants, she’s the rich perfect princess always striving to live up to everyone’s expectations. He’s tortured every week when she picks him up and directs looks of disgust his way. Add to that misery is having to sit through Sunday brunch with a family that blames him for his brother’s death. He’s always been the black sheep of the family but Remy’s death has strained their relationship to the breaking point. <br /><br />Things get interesting when Rule finally wakes up and notices Shaw. He knows starting something with her won’t be like his string of skanks. He knows and has a history with her, so it won’t be a one night stand, but he can’t stay away. Shaw can’t resist Rule even realizing there’s a strong possibility their relationship will crash and burn, she still can’t help but take the chance. She’s tired of living safe and doing what her parents expect when they’ve never paid no mind to her. <br /><br />Knowing Shaw had feelings for Rule for ages made my heart break for her. I always want unrequited love to get noticed and returned, so it was very satisfying to see this come about. I loved the passion and intensity both Rule and Shaw showed to each other, and I liked seeing Rule figure out what he was missing all these years. There were lots of smoking hot scenes and sizzling chemistry that were such fun to read. Plus, there was suspense that had you clicking through the pages worrying about what would happen next. That was one crazy ex! <br /><br />I’m so glad I picked this up because it was exactly what I was in the mood for. Now I’m eagerly looking forward to Jet and Ayden’s story. <br /><br />Thanks for the giggles and gossip, Bethany, Laura and Jenn! <br /><br />You can find this review and more at <a href="http://thereadersden.blogspot.com/2013/02/review-rule-by-jay-crownover.html" rel="nofollow noopener">The Readers Den. </a><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="17792339682497245390" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer496125902" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer12535559848505420189"><b>100 stars!!!!<br/><br/>DING DING DING!!!<br/><br/>AND WE HAVE ANOTHER WINNER! ^_^ </b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380403640ra/785286.gif' width='400' height='350' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380403640i/785287.jpg' width='400' height='230' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380403640ra/785288.gif' width='400' height='340' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/><br/>Honestly, this is one of the best bad boy meets good girl books! He dresses the part too, complete with the mohawk and crazy hair colors. He lives his life the way he wants to and that's always how it has been. Rule may look like and act like the world's big</span>
  <span id="freeText12535559848505420189" style="display:none"><b>100 stars!!!!<br><br>DING DING DING!!!<br><br>AND WE HAVE ANOTHER WINNER! ^_^ </b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380403640ra/785286.gif" width="400" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380403640i/785287.jpg" width="400" height="230" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380403640ra/785288.gif" width="400" height="340" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br>Honestly, this is one of the best bad boy meets good girl books! I recommend it to everyone. Let's all read this! <br><br>The story is all about our hero, RULE. He's every mom's nightmare. He has so many tattoos since he's also a tattoo artist himself. He dresses the part too, complete with the mohawk and crazy hair colors. He lives his life the way he wants to and that's always how it has been. Rule may look like and act like the world's biggest badass, but he has his demons. His twin brother died 3 years ago and his mom blamed him for it. Even though he was always second best to his twin, they had a good family back then, and now they didn't. Their mom is practically batshit crazy now because she's (as Shaw says) rewriting an imaginary history wherein Rule is the villain. As expected, Rule didn't take this lightly. In fact, he always doubts people's feelings for him. They always gotta prove that they care for him. <br><br>Enters our heroine princess, Shaw. Yes, I'll call her princess, and that's a real compliment because she's just too good to be true! I mean, I love her character because hell yeah, she's rich, but she's not a snob. She doesn't rub her money on another person's face. She's very patient with everyone, she's kind, loyal, headstrong and she loves as hard as she can. She has been in love with Rule ever since she was 13. Unfortunately, Remy, Rule's twin, used her as a pseudo-girlfriend in the eyes of the Archer family <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ since he was gay and didn't wanna come out  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> so Rule has been seeing her only as his brother's girl. LOL. <br><br>One night, sparks fly and suddenly, Rule is looking at her in a different way. He was even willing to KINDA date her, which was in his case, such a big deal because he didn't really date. Rule knows that a relationship with Shaw changes everything and she couldn't be just one of "those girls". On the other hand, Shaw has been struggling because she couldn't tell Rule that she loved him... A LOT. And that's where the complications rise. It was beautiful, even with the complications. I love how the author showed both of their imperfections. I love how their redeeming qualities also showed after everything. I love how Rule has been taught by Shaw that he could be loved just like everyone else.<br><br>This novel not only shows how two completely different people could totally fall for each other, it also shows how people deal with grief, and that is a beautiful thing because it's proof that we're all human. Rule's mom admitted something in the end and that made a whole lot of a difference for my Rule. I just bet he needed that the most! <br><br>The ending was really good. I love their getting-back-together scene! It rocked and y'all should look forward to it! ^_^ <br><br>So that's it.. ANOTHER WINNER FOR ME!<br><br><b>I applaud for this book! I LOVE IT! ^_^</b></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/502248799" />
    <a title="Smitten&#39;s Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog"><img alt="Smitten&#39;s Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1429608146p2/12994342.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/502248799?book_show_action=true">Jan 10, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Smitten&#39;s Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Smitten&#39;s Book Blog" href="/user/show/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog">Smitten&#39;s Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=steamy-reads">steamy-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=bad-boy">bad-boy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=men-with-ink">men-with-ink</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=friends-to-lovers">friends-to-lovers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=virginal-heroine">virginal-heroine</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer502248799" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8817568152636124706"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380404540i/787277._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380404540i/787278._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>(Use necessary imagination to add appropriate piercings, tattoos, hair colour etc.)<br/><br/><b>Rule</b><br/><i>/ro͞ol/</i><br/>Noun<br/>A generalized statement that describes what is true in most or all cases.<br/>Verb<br/>- To dominate by powerful influence.<br/>- Slang; To be excellent or superior<br/><br/>Well well well. How can you not love Rule?!<br/><br/><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"It's genetically impossible not to be kind of in love with him when you come equipped with a vagina."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br/><br/>My God, this book turned me on, made me cry and made me smile! I love a book like that!<br/><br/>Before I </span>
  <span id="freeText8817568152636124706" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380404540i/787277._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380404540i/787278._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>(Use necessary imagination to add appropriate piercings, tattoos, hair colour etc.)<br><br><b>Rule</b><br><i>/ro͞ol/</i><br>Noun<br>A generalized statement that describes what is true in most or all cases.<br>Verb<br>- To dominate by powerful influence.<br>- Slang; To be excellent or superior<br><br>Well well well. How can you not love Rule?!<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"It's genetically impossible not to be kind of in love with him when you come equipped with a vagina."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>My God, this book turned me on, made me cry and made me smile! I love a book like that!<br><br>Before I go on, I need to mention... the typos are appalling. Lol. There are spelling errors, sentences that run on and on and with no punctuation and words inserted where they shouldn't be. But I hear that there is an edited version coming out, and if you can ignore it, this is a fantastic read! It's worth ignoring the grammatical mistakes.<br><br>Aaaah, Rule Rule Rule. Hot, tattooed-to-within-an-inch-of-his-life, pierced, angsty badass. Aaaand there's the small matter of the apadravya! (Don't know what that is? Get your ass on Google right now!) *fans self* <br>Rule lives his life making sure he is the <i>exception</i> to the <i>rule</i>, 'A generalized statement that describes what is true in most or all cases', decorating his skin with an array of colourful ink and determined to be his own man. A man that knows his own mind and is as different as different can be from his late and painfully missed, perfect twin brother, Remy.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"I don't care what color your hair is, if you're pale or tan, if you have makeup on or just work up all I care about is that when I look at you, you always look back and see me."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>But there is no denying, he <i>rules</i> in every sense of the word;<br>'Slang; To be excellent or superior' and 'To dominate by powerful influence', where Shaw is concerned. She's loved him forever and just needs him to open his eyes and realise it.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"It's always been you even when I didn't want it to be, even when it broke my heart over and over again. It's just always been you."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>I love stories where the characters have known each other for ever and eventually get it together. There's something about the intimacy and connection that only a complicated history can add to a relationship.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"I've never trusted anyone all the time. It's the people I care about the most that always seem to do the most damage."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>Shaw was a fantastic heroine. I really warmed to her. I felt for her, where her parents were concerned, but she was still a strong, independent, intelligent female lead.<br><br>As I mentioned, you can't not love Rule. He's clearly chewed up over the loss of his twin brother and the break down of his family, but you can see from the beginning that there is a good man underneath all the metal, tats and brooding. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"You have to promise not to bail on me when I get lost, Shaw. You have to promise to just wait it out until I can find my way back. I need to know you're at the end of the tunnel when everything goes black."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>Jay Crownover is fab at writing from his POV. The easy, chatty, slang and typically male take on things was brilliant to read. There was a lot of fun and comedy in the book. The dialogue was flowing and witty and, despite the typos, it all made reading this book so easy.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"I almost saw your boyfriend naked this morning."<br>I laughed at the look on her face. "I don't know what to say to that, you're welcome?"</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>Shaw and Rule are polar opposites to the casual observer. She's the angel to his devil and the light to his dark. But underneath, they have more in common than even they realise.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Opposites don't just attract they freaking catch fire and burn the entire city down."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380404541i/787279._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The book is super hot and the sexual chemistry between Shaw and Rule is scrumptious! <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Tell me why when we do this it's so much different than whenever I've done it before."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>Surrounding characters were great. I adored Rome and hope he features in future books, and I can't wait to read about Jet and Ayden. You could feel the author building the extended cast to set each of them up for their own stories and I love that.<br><br>And to finish, I have nothing more to say other than... Best closing line ever! <i>So</i> Rule!<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>Look at me being all optimistic and shit. <br>Remy would be so proud.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380404541i/787280._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>To read more reviews go to my Book Blog: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://smittensbookblog.wordpress.com/">http://smittensbookblog.wordpress.com/</a><br>Follow me on Twitter: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://twitter.com/SmittenSC">https://twitter.com/SmittenSC</a><br>Find me on Pinterest: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://pinterest.com/smittensc/">http://pinterest.com/smittensc/</a><br>Join in the chat on Facebook: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.facebook.com/groups/427743250626754/?fref=ts">http://www.facebook.com/groups/427743...</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="8817568152636124706" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_493351295" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/493351295" />
    <a title="SueBee★bring me an alpha!★" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/15735368-suebee-bring-me-an-alpha"><img alt="SueBee★bring me an alpha!★" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1528597635p2/15735368.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/493351295?book_show_action=true">Jan 02, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="SueBee★bring me an alpha!★" class="user" itemprop="url" name="SueBee★bring me an alpha!★" href="/user/show/15735368-suebee-bring-me-an-alpha">SueBee★bring me an alpha!★</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15735368-suebee-bring-me-an-alpha?shelf=series-g-contemporaries">series-g-contemporaries</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15735368-suebee-bring-me-an-alpha?shelf=series-cr-stand-alone">series-cr-stand-alone</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15735368-suebee-bring-me-an-alpha?shelf=series-check-on-sequel">series-check-on-sequel</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15735368-suebee-bring-me-an-alpha?shelf=kindle">kindle</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15735368-suebee-bring-me-an-alpha?shelf=read-stand-alones-cr">read-stand-alones-cr</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15735368-suebee-bring-me-an-alpha?shelf=read-contemporaries">read-contemporaries</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15735368-suebee-bring-me-an-alpha?shelf=g-contemporaries">g-contemporaries</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15735368-suebee-bring-me-an-alpha?shelf=heroes-bad-boy">heroes-bad-boy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15735368-suebee-bring-me-an-alpha?shelf=4-and-half-stars">4-and-half-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15735368-suebee-bring-me-an-alpha?shelf=heroes-favs-modern">heroes-favs-modern</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer493351295" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10364494799365375257"><a href='http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/CrownoverRule1TitlebySueBee_zpsa359a90d.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1388987707i/7966731.jpg' alt=' photo CrownoverRule1TitlebySueBee_zpsa359a90d.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><a href='http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/GIF%20Sexy%20embrace/tattooembracebysb_zps1c2fa456.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1388987707ra/7966732.gif' alt=' photo tattooembracebysb_zps1c2fa456.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><b>★★★★1/2! Rule series, book 1 (stand-alone). Debut by Jay Crownover. Oh so troubled rebel & a girl who’s tired of always being the good girl.</b><br/><br/><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“I adore Rule. I think it’s genetically impossible not to be kind of in love with him when you come equipped with a vagina. It’s just something about all that angsty, moody swagger he has that makes you want to cuddle him up and make him feel better.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br/><u>Books in the Marked Men series are stand-alones, but most enjoyed if read in </u></span>
  <span id="freeText10364494799365375257" style="display:none"><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/CrownoverRule1TitlebySueBee_zpsa359a90d.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1388987707i/7966731.jpg" alt=" photo CrownoverRule1TitlebySueBee_zpsa359a90d.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/GIF%20Sexy%20embrace/tattooembracebysb_zps1c2fa456.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1388987707ra/7966732.gif" alt=" photo tattooembracebysb_zps1c2fa456.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>★★★★1/2! Rule series, book 1 (stand-alone). Debut by Jay Crownover. Oh so troubled rebel &amp; a girl who’s tired of always being the good girl.</b><br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“I adore Rule. I think it’s genetically impossible not to be kind of in love with him when you come equipped with a vagina. It’s just something about all that angsty, moody swagger he has that makes you want to cuddle him up and make him feel better.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br><u>Books in the Marked Men series are stand-alones, but most enjoyed if read in order.</u><br><b>Book 1: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/493351295" rel="nofollow noopener">Rule</a><br>Book 2: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/495735832" rel="nofollow noopener">Jet</a><br>Book 3: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/590322738" rel="nofollow noopener">Rome</a><br>Book 4: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/813893586" rel="nofollow noopener">Nash</a><br>Book 5: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/813893614" rel="nofollow noopener">Rowdy</a><br>Book 6: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/813893628" rel="nofollow noopener">Asa</a></b><br><i>
  <b><br><a>RULE ARCHER:</a> 22 years old/tattoo artist/twin/dark brown hair/light blue-grey eyes.</b>
</i><br><br><b>Rule first met Shaw</b> when he was sixteen and she was barely fourteen years old. Shaw had become best friends with Rule’s twin brother, Remy. All the years since everyone had thought Remy and Shaw a couple, but they never were. Then just three years prior Remy tragically died in a car accident while en route to pick up his drunk brother Rule. Remy’s death devastated the Archer family and Shaw. Remy’s mother is still grasping with her loss and blaming Rule (she is sort of the villain of this book, if you ask me!). <br><i>
  <b><br><a>SHAW LANDON, “Casper”:</a> 19 years old/student-aspiring emergency doctor-waitress-heiress/light blond hair/green eyes/virgin.</b>
</i><br><br><b>Shaw fell in love with Rule</b> from the moment they first met and she has been harboring a secret crush ever since. But Shaw is so different from Rule. She is very much the good girl, at the same time she feels boxed in by this persona. Even though her wealthy parents have been very detached she continues to try to please them. She is a student with good grades with aspirations of becoming an emergency room doctor. She is the sweetest most thoughtful, smart and very endearing heroine, but somewhere inside of her there is a wilder side trying to break out. She never had many friends, except for Remy and more recently her roommate Ayden (book 2). Rule’s and Remy’s family had become her surrogate family and she was very close to everyone, well maybe except Rule. At the age of nineteen she has pretty much given up any hope that Rule will ever see her for more than Remy’s girl if even that…<br><br>Rule - the too handsome rebel, the troubled, tortured and self-destructive hero, the black sheep of his family lives with his roommate Nash in the city (Denver) and works at a tattoo parlor. His life pretty much comes down to avoiding his mother at as much as possible, working, partying with his friends Nash (roommate), Jet (book 2) and Rowdy, bringing home a different girl each night AND kicking her out in the morning.<br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“I was viscerally aware that the majority of my time was spent trying to outrun the shadow of my dead twin. I wallowed in superficial relationships so no one could get close to me, no one could judge me and find me lacking.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br>Rule never, at least consciously, saw Shaw for anything other than a family friend and Remy’s girlfriend. He can recognize that she is stunningly beautiful, but she is too preppy and proper:<br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“She was the kind of girl that guys looked at, just because they couldn’t help themselves, but as soon as she turned those frosty green eyes in their direction they knew they wouldn’t stand a chance. She exuded unattainability the way some other girls oozed ‘come and get me’.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br>Well that is until the moment Rule truly notices Shaw and realizes that there is more to Shaw than meets the eye – Rule’s wake-up moment:<br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“He was leaning back against the door watching me with hooded eyes. He wasn’t throwing sarcastic barbs at me or ignoring me, he was just watching me.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br>Fortunately for us this is just the beginning of Rule’s and Shaw’s story. Buckle up for this is one bumpy ride of unresolved family issues, well-kept secrets, stalkers and much more as these two very different yet emotionally starved souls get to know each other. It is very much a journey for Rule and Shaw coming to terms with who they are and where they fit into this world.<br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“I wasn’t the type that got jealous, I mean I lived my entire life not being as good as my twin, so I couldn’t understand the murderous rage that was suddenly flowing through me, the sudden need to claim something, to announce to the world that she was mine...”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br>This story is alternating between Rule’s and Shaw’s POV. Ms. Crownover did a terrific job giving us Rules and Shaw’s story. She is an amazing story teller! You may have noticed comments from early reviewers about edits being needed. I read the 2nd edition and I only spotted a few – nothing that affected my rating of this wonderful read!<br><br>***<br>Hero rating: 4.5 stars <br>Heroine rating: 4 stars<br>Sex scenes rating: 4.5 stars<br>Sex scenes frequency: 4 stars<br>Storyline concept rating: 5 stars<br>Storytelling skills rating: 5 stars<br>Story ending rating: 4.5 stars<br>Book editing rating (5 = no edits spotted): 4.5 stars<br>******************************<br><b>Overall rating: 4.5 stars<br><br>Would I recommend this series: Yes.<br>Would I re-read this series: Maybe later.<br>Would I read future books by this author: Yes.</b><br><br><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/GIF%20Heroes/tattooartbysb_zpsf703e298.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1388987707ra/7966733.gif" alt=" photo tattooartbysb_zpsf703e298.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="10364494799365375257" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_505112941" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/505112941" />
    <a title="SheReadsALot" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6270231-shereadsalot"><img alt="SheReadsALot" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1516045546p2/6270231.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/505112941?book_show_action=true">Jan 13, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="SheReadsALot" class="user" itemprop="url" name="SheReadsALot" href="/user/show/6270231-shereadsalot">SheReadsALot</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6270231-shereadsalot?shelf=bad-boy">bad-boy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6270231-shereadsalot?shelf=angst">angst</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6270231-shereadsalot?shelf=part-of-a-series">part-of-a-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6270231-shereadsalot?shelf=player-or-man-whore">player-or-man-whore</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6270231-shereadsalot?shelf=virgin">virgin</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6270231-shereadsalot?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6270231-shereadsalot?shelf=artist-or-artsy-type">artist-or-artsy-type</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6270231-shereadsalot?shelf=piercing-down-there">piercing-down-there</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6270231-shereadsalot?shelf=damaged-hero">damaged-hero</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer505112941" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17074436307943833330"><b>WARNING: This story has typos. A lot. And if you're a stickler, you might not be too enthused. Oh and there's the age and years past discrepancy, Shaw supposedly met the Archer family at 13 and has known them for eight years and in the book, at present time, Shaw is 19 going on 20. Do we see the issue with the math? Yes? Okay then. </b><br/><br/>There are plenty of reviews commenting on the editing needs of this story. However, this is one of the stories where all that shit...it can actually take a back burne</span>
  <span id="freeText17074436307943833330" style="display:none"><b>WARNING: This story has typos. A lot. And if you're a stickler, you might not be too enthused. Oh and there's the age and years past discrepancy, Shaw supposedly met the Archer family at 13 and has known them for eight years and in the book, at present time, Shaw is 19 going on 20. Do we see the issue with the math? Yes? Okay then. </b><br><br>There are plenty of reviews commenting on the editing needs of this story. However, this is one of the stories where all that shit...it can actually take a back burner. And I'm letting this slide-for the most part. I mean pulling someone's skin <i>taunt</i>, it irked me a little reading it the<i> second time</i>. But I'm going to let it go. <br><br>Why?<br><br>Read my words: The story is that good. I'm only taking away 1/2 star, it's a 4.5 winner. <br><br>So.<br><br>Rule. (Granted Rule doesn't smoke but he's tatted up the wazoo so this pic is closer to how I envisioned than the cover)<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380404958i/788391._SY540_.jpg" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><br>Yes.<br><br>Hmm...<br><br>He's everything I love when reading a hero, he's a bad boy, doesn't mind scrapping when the time calls, tattooed, <i>pierced!</i> (<b>Apadrayva &amp; Jacob's Ladder heaven</b> - I was in raptures) and is crazy about his girl. But he's damaged and angsty and agro and just...delicious. And one owner of an ironic name albeit cool name. Rule. *giggles* He doesn't follow them, he makes them and breaks them!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/244684.gif" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br> <br>*middle fingers to the world* Don't you just love it?<br><br>And Shaw? Also a possessor of a cool name. (As a matter of fact, this author gets kudos for the name choices - the Archer boys do sound like Street Fighter characters - Rome, Rule and Remy- but it's all good)She's not annoying!!! And <b>not</b> a TSTL heroine. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/427994.gif" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>It's a joyous state of affairs when you have to not call out the heroine for being a whiny, snot nosed wimp who couldn't think for herself. Shaw has a brain. But more importantly she used it. (Alright there were some sketchy moments but knowing her background of trying to have her parents' approval I can understand her warped decisions) But whatever man, I'm over looking the minor niggle of doubt, she's pretty solid and not that bad when I recall my TSTL Hall of Fame.<br><br>There's a crazy ex-stalker, excellent secondary characters with possible lead stories in the future(I hope), angsty family drama and secrets revealed, dark and sad themes on family neglect/grief/ acceptance and within all of that...a damn love story. <br><br>Was it an epic love story? <br><br>Nope. <br><br>But pretty close.<br><br>What sold me was the more realistic approach Shaw and Rule had to there issues. They had to put in work to have their happy ending. And I appreciate stories like that.<br><br>I'm anxious for the next in the series (though I am a bit put out it's Jet and not Rome but as long as Rome gets a story, I'm gravy baby)<br><br>This story continued my excellent mood, I'm like in a unicorn shitting rainbows, happy good mood!!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380404958i/788392.jpg" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b>FOUR &amp; A HALF STARS</b><br><br>So...<img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380404958ra/788393.gif" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="17074436307943833330" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

He was one hell of a character and I just LOVED him!!!<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380404231i/786528.jpg' width='300' height='300' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Meet <b>Shaw Landon</b>...beautiful, medical school bound, daugther of prominent parents and longtime Archer family friend.   <span id="freeText9266877042882076628" style="display:none"><b>4 1/2 Tattooed Stars!!!</b><br><br>Yes there were many grammatical errors…but I loved the story enough to see past it! (Kinda like Shaw saw past Rule’s tattoos and piercings.)<br><br>Meet <b>Rule Archer</b>...pierced, tattooed, explosive personality, man-whore, loyal, hard-worker, black sheep of his family and newest addition to my book boyfriend list. <span id="freeTextContainer12834491133353475852">Self confessed Romance addict here, Throwing out stars as I happily smile my way through this book. I was all kinds of in love, heartbroken and swoony with this 5 star beauty. What can be sweeter than a story about two people (soul mates) who finally find a way to make each other whole.<br/><br/>Meet Tattooed, misunderstand Rule and beautiful, strong shaw. A story of opposites attract and all the juicy bits in between. I loved the plot, the characters (main and supporting), the romance, the angst, the hea</span>
  <span id="freeText12834491133353475852" style="display:none">Self confessed Romance addict here, Throwing out stars as I happily smile my way through this book. I was all kinds of in love, heartbroken and swoony with this 5 star beauty. What can be sweeter than a story about two people (soul mates) who finally find a way to make each other whole.<br /><br />Meet Tattooed, misunderstand Rule and beautiful, strong shaw. A story of opposites attract and all the juicy bits in between. I loved the plot, the characters (main and supporting), the romance, the angst, the heartache most of all I loved sharing this journey. *sigh* I don't think I've read a book with so many amazingly named characters (Rule, Shaw, Remy, Rome, Jet, Ayden) need I go on ... ?<br /><br />This story grabbed my attention and my heart and I thoroughly was delighted from beginning to end (yes some errors throughout, but why complain you get to read about Rule - TUT)! <br /><br />so did I love? - oh yes<br />Would I recommend? - give it a bash<br />Am I in love with a fictional character once again - sigh!<br />Will I ever tire of Romance - NEVER<br /><br />Read the blurb for the book it says it all.<br /><br />4 bad boy tattoos stars.<br /><br />Ps author can we please have a story about Rome?</span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28146945-sara-ink-is-my-sword?shelf=addictive">addictive</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28146945-sara-ink-is-my-sword?shelf=eyeroll">eyeroll</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28146945-sara-ink-is-my-sword?shelf=buddy-reads">buddy-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28146945-sara-ink-is-my-sword?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28146945-sara-ink-is-my-sword?shelf=forgetable">forgetable</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1311701967" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11533198216408025041"><b>1 “Hilariously infuriating & Hilariously absurd” Stars</b><br/><br/><i>“I won’t even bother with a quote”</i><br/><br/><b> Buddy read with <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/48727754-chandler-ainsley-reads' rel='nofollow noopener'>my beautiful partner in crime of NA books.</a> We both hated this book so yeah it was an awesome bonding experience. </b><br/><br/>I can totally see why I enjoyed reading this when I was 14. I mean I was young I didn't know more, and hot bad guys were my optimal crush. BUT NOW I KNOW MORE SO I WILL NOT ACCEPT THIS. <br/><br/><i>I have such a strong hatred for this book that it interrupted my train of thought while walking </i></span>
  <span id="freeText11533198216408025041" style="display:none"><b>1 “Hilariously infuriating &amp; Hilariously absurd” Stars</b><br /><br /><i>“I won’t even bother with a quote”</i><br /><br /><b> Buddy read with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/48727754-chandler-ainsley-reads" rel="nofollow noopener">my beautiful partner in crime of NA books.</a> We both hated this book so yeah it was an awesome bonding experience. </b><br /><br />I can totally see why I enjoyed reading this when I was 14. I mean I was young I didn't know more, and hot bad guys were my optimal crush. BUT NOW I KNOW MORE SO I WILL NOT ACCEPT THIS. <br /><br /><i>I have such a strong hatred for this book that it interrupted my train of thought while walking upstairs and I may have fallen. Hmph.</i> <br /><br /><b>Things I liked:</b><s> Oh my, I struggled with this one a lot. Let’s just get over with this.</s> <br /><br />-Side characters. Kind of. I mean I am actually interested in the story but not very optimistic that I would like the books more. This is funny because I already read this series but I don’t remember anything.<br />-Cool concept of following tattoo artists.<br /><br />So I really wanted to at least say this had been an addictive trashy read, but I surprised myself when I was really bored and trying to skim read. So yeah it was not addictive whatsoever.<br /><br /><b>Things I hated:</b> EVERYTHING. <br /><br />Now if you want to continue reading this review know I will be touching upon specific scenes so it may be quite <b>spoilery.</b> <br /><br />So I will probably be saying bye-bye to some of you. I honestly don’t care if you do read it or not, is your reading taste your life whatever. <b>You do YOU, I do I and I will trash this book I am not sorry. </b><br /><br /><b>WARNING: </b>From now on I will be using strong language, probably will ramble and be overly exasperated and angry.<br /><br />Okay, first you just need to know this two basic thoughts. Rule is redeemable just because he is compared with a stalker-psycho-rich-preppy-dude. Meaning he was not redeemable. So if you are waiting for this dark dude with a huge heavy past where you can’t help but protect it, this is not your guy. Second, Shaw was smart until she was not, she may be the most stupid character I have ever encountered in NA. <br /><br />P.S. This book teaches you that if you treat women well you are basically a giant pussy. So fuck, excuse me but I hope all men are giant pussies then. <br /><br /><b>Rule: FUCK HE WAS AN ASSHOLE, TRULY.</b> And I am for sure not insulting him when every three pages he reminded us he was one, literally. There is no fucked up past to redeem him, he has been a bad guy since forever. Sure your mom is trash as well but that doesn’t mean you can try other women and people like trash. Why do I make an emphasis on women? Because he was horrible to very much only women. I usually give no fuck in terms of characters sexual activity, but if you are gonna be having sex with a woman every single weekend and you are not worried you are carrying STD’s, I am judging you. He was an utter shit with all the women he spent a night with, we are not asking you to tell them you loved them, is just common decency, my dude. He literally looked at women as if they were meat or ice cream, different flavors easy to have his way with. Do I need to remind everyone that the first night he was out after declaring his “somehow-relationship” with Shaw he could keep his eyes off other women? Like not just scanning how hot they were, but saying over and over again how he would love to have sex with them. BURN JUST BURN. But of course, he didn’t have a problem with making Shaw feel like a utter shit for riding to a meeting with his ex, even knowing she had zero attraction to him. UGHH. Mmmmm, he also has serious problems with violence. <s>I am tired to pretend white-straight-dudes saying they wanna kill people is totally fine because if a poc were to say the same, they would be treated as gang members, a total danger for people, so yes I had to bring race right here because is true. Fight me if you want to.</s><br /><br /><b>Shawn:</b> My dear, you were plainly stupid. Why? Because when the guy of your dreams, the asshole of your life, started treating you finally with decency you fucking hated it. So yeap I am not even blaming him to be horrible with you because you fucking loved it? Basically, you let him treat you like shit, made you feel like shit, but you secretly just wanted more. Emmm… sure you were a bit sassy and all that jazz but you were also a horrible person with anyone who was interested in Rule.All your problems somehow always turned to Rule, you could be dealing with your family stuff or your post trauma after the assault but always ended up on Rule. Like fuck why?<br /><br />Basically, this two characters felt they were the shit.com. Supermodels who turned heads every time they walked everywhere and then the people who turned were sluts. <b>BYE. <br /><br />Family:</b> All families were a piece of crap. All families were horrible.They were obviously made to receive hate, and that’s exactly what I am doing. Now, the mom of the Archer boys, was the cherry on top of hypocrisy. She could very much be abandoned by everyone and wouldn’t have felt a bit of sympathy. <br /><br /><b>Slut-shaming:</b> WELL THIS IS A PRETTY BIG NORMAL THING YOU DO IN THIS BOOK, so probably need to be okay with this, because if not you will want to pull out every single hair of your head by the end of the story. If I follow the rule of this book, slut/tramp/bambi, is everyone who appeared even a bit interested in our main guy. But Let me tell you if I were to slut-shame anyone here it would have been RULE. <s>Like fuck, why having testicles, or identifying as a male immediately saves you from being called a slut. When you are obviously the one who has sex with pretty much everyone and also eat everyone with their eyes. </s> It was obvious that the purpose of making other female characters who wanted Rule was too called them bambies, they were there just for that purpose.<br /><br /><b>Using LGBTQIA characters as a plot device:</b> Excuse me but this has gotten old. Like the poor guy couldn’t even defend himself because he was dead. Like bro, why he not screaming to the four winds he was homosexual was such a big trouble. Literally, his parents knew and they preferred to act as if it didn’t exist. I DIDN’T LIKE THIS. <br /><br /><b>Sex-scenes:</b> BORINGGG AND DUBIOUS. First sex interaction they had, she was completely wasted, which probably would indicate you that her decision-making ability wasn’t clear. Rule kept repeating that a decent guy wouldn’t touch someone in this states, yet he proceeds to do so, so yeah an asshole. May I also remind that at that moment Shawn was still his brother's girlfriend. He just accepted her because he found her hot after seeing her wearing a tiny sports uniform, for fuck's sake. The other sexy-times were just meh. I mean yeah sure it was cool to read about people with metal alterations in their private parts but that’s about it.<br /><br /><b>Relationship:</b> I will call this emotionally-abusive. Lets’ just summit up like this: Rule fucked up + Shaw felt responsible for it = Shaw saying sorry and make-up sex.<br /><br />As I made clear I HATED THIS BOOK. No, I don't regret reading it because it has helped me open my eyes in how much I have changed as a person, and I for sure it for better.</span>
  <a data-text-id="11533198216408025041" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1331871797?book_show_action=true">Jul 11, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1331871797" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3981512426978585865"><b>Actual rating: 0.5/5 disappointing star</b><br/><br/><u>Plot/Setting</u><br/>In my opinion, the main characters, aka <i>Rule</i> and <i>Shaw</i>, had way too much more conversations <b>in bed</b> <s>during sex</s> than anywhere "normal." Typically that doesn't bother me in New Adult books, but this one definitely goes out of control on those scenes. Believe me, you'll find they were having another forbidden fruit every a few(like, two) chapters since they experienced their first time from chapter 5. The biggest problem about the whole book is <b>its l</b></span>
  <span id="freeText3981512426978585865" style="display:none"><b>Actual rating: 0.5/5 disappointing star</b><br /><br /><u>Plot/Setting</u><br />In my opinion, the main characters, aka <i>Rule</i> and <i>Shaw</i>, had way too much more conversations <b>in bed</b> <s>during sex</s> than anywhere "normal." Typically that doesn't bother me in New Adult books, but this one definitely goes out of control on those scenes. Believe me, you'll find they were having another forbidden fruit every a few(like, two) chapters since they experienced their first time from chapter 5. The biggest problem about the whole book is <b>its lack of commas</b> in between paragraphs and the sentences. I know I'm probably not the first person to point this out, but seriously, I was surprised that it wasn't some printing mistakes, it was actually printed that way. I needed to control my instant desire to put some commas in it all the time.<br /><br /><u>Characters</u><br />I used to love bad boys; however, the kind like <b>Rule</b> is too peculiar to accept. He was a trouble maker, I got it, but his appearance and the way he decorated himself made me really uncomfortable. Imagine kissing a guy with lips and tongue piercings(I think I'll be worrying too much about whether touching him is painful or accidentally pull on those...holes) or trying to find a clean and skin-colored place on his body but couldn't spot one because it was colorfully tattooed. Let me make this clear, I always appreciate those artworks in reality, but no offense, it's hard to put myself <i>in the story</i> under such circumstances.<br /><br /><u>Overall</u><br />In short, this book isn't for me so as a result, <b>I won't recommend it to anyone.</b> Although it has a high average score of 4.17/5 <s>unbelievable</s> stars, I wasn't able to capture the meaningful essence in Rule and Shaw's story.</span>

		    <b>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('GdNlrSEyx+iSyRWrnsEAC//2ntRjMdEGmdWnRnJaTXfgH9jtOaItFkVF3o2XLuCs7/hEcDQ2igRyxLt8MAwmdQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('vevs5CSOqmWsfHge3SPJJ4/EwCIB2TOSKACzC/qsjXVEJ1GkPB5Am3vwszjUzCmAn8oahlbeaJDDEa8xuPrmdw==')})
  }

  <span id="freeText13429548443816617024" style="display:none">Jay Crownover is the International and multiple New York Times and USA Today bestselling author of the Marked Men Series, The Saints of Denver Series, and The Point and Breaking Point Series. Her books can be found translated in many different languages all around the world. She is a tattooed, crazy haired Colorado native who lives at the base of the Rockies with her awesome dogs. This is where she can frequently be found enjoying a cold beer and Taco Tuesdays. Jay is a self-declared music snob and outspoken book lover who is always looking for her next adventure, between the pages and on the road.<br />GUYS!!!
